data-v-ed53bdfc><section class="TopSection center-content" data-v-5f9a7353><div class="Left" data-v-5f9a7353><div data-v-5f9a7353>  <div ssr-only data-v-ff36072c data-v-ff36072c data-v-5f9a7353><h2 data-v-ff36072c>README</h2> <div class="MarkdownView readme-markdown-view" data-v-6e6eb3be data-v-ff36072c><div class="MarkdownPreview" data-v-6e6eb3be><h2>Overview</h2>
<h1>VIN Decoder</h1>
<p>It takes a vin number and decodes it! It’s free for 100 api calls per month.</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>It support All Vin Decoding for North America</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>We added support for Asian/Europe VIN Numbers as well (Beta Phase)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The Vin decoder API supports Motorcycle/Boat/Bike Decoding as well</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Our Api can perform Salvage Title Check, you can retrieve images, and salvage title information from our api</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p>These are the api used to power our <a href="https://www.vinfreecheck.com/salvage-check" rel="noopener noreferrer external nofollow ugc" target="_blank">https://www.vinfreecheck.com/salvage-check</a> and <a href="https://www.vinfreecheck.com/vin-decoder" rel="noopener noreferrer external nofollow ugc" target="_blank">Free VIN Decoder</a></p>
<p>For more information check it out at: <a href="https://www.vinfreecheck.com/vin-decoding-api" rel="noopener noreferrer external nofollow ugc" target="_blank">Vin Decoding API</a></p>
